name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

msg:Address: After getting off the highway, there is a sign on the roadside not far away. Turn into the small road and there are two parking lots. The big parking lot is a bit far from the hotel, and the small one can't park a few cars. All the cars are parked on the roadside near the hotel.

Service: I arrived at almost 2 o'clock in the afternoon, but the room was not ready for check-in. I waited for more than half an hour before the room was ready for check-in. The attitude of the front desk staff was okay, but not very professional. The overall hotel did not experience the service quality that matched the price.

Room: We booked Japanese tatami that can be soaked indoors. The overall decoration is relatively old. Many of them have cracked, bulged, and discolored. The faucets and showers are also leaking on the sides. The only thing I am satisfied with is that the mattress is not bad. The central air conditioner will turn on automatically at night when I sleep, and the noise is still quite loud.

Hot spring: The hot spring time is until 11pm. We went there at 8pm. We changed into swimsuits in the room. The floor of the bathing area in the men's locker room was very dirty. I don't know if it was mud or hair. Many drains were blocked by hair. The shower water flow was relatively small, and some were broken. It was very cold after washing. There was no heating. There was only a gas heater at the door of the locker room. When you enter the indoor bathing area, you can smell the water vapor mixed with the smell of paint. The color of the water in the pool is also dark, with mud at the bottom. There are also many impurities in the outdoor water. The overall experience is not good. I didn't feel like soaking and went back to the room directly without going to the entertainment area.

Breakfast: Simple buffet, two points I want to complain about, one is that the fried dough sticks are obviously leftover, and they are very hard to bite after heating, and the second is that there are no glasses in the hot drink area in the restaurant after 8 o'clock, so you can only use paper cups. The taste of other meals is average.

Overall evaluation: The hotel facilities are old, the dynamic line is strange, the decoration is rough, the service is amateur, and the experience is extremely poor. The price was over 1,300 RMB when I booked it before the Chinese New Year, but it had risen to over 1,600 RMB on the day. What I was most dissatisfied with was that after spending so much money, the overall experience was totally not worth the price. I chose the most expensive one in Bazhou at that time, thinking that spending more money would always have its own reasons, but I was totally ripped off.

msg:First of all, the geographical location is 1 hour and 30 minutes drive from Beijing, which is quite convenient. We arrived on Friday night and went to soak in the outdoor hot springs first. They were still under repair, and an excavator was parked around the pool. It was simply... There are about 5-6 outdoor hot springs, and the water temperature is around 40 degrees, which is still very comfortable. Apart from the construction factors, it is still very suitable for watching the moon at night. There is a private hot spring pool indoors, which is about 1.5 meters long and 1.2 meters wide. It can be bigger. The water quality and environment are very good, but the sound of the central air conditioner is like driving an old tractor, rumbling and making people unable to sleep. When sleeping, you can only turn it off and spend a night on the switch. I thought I could sleep until 12 o'clock, but I didn't expect that the decoration would start before 8 o'clock in the morning. The sound of electric drills and hammers, squeaking, booming, and booming, I had to coordinate with the hotel customer service 3 times before it stopped. I couldn't sleep, so I went to have breakfast. The breakfast is free when you check in, and the variety is very rich. I really want to give a thumbs up here. But the table in a good restaurant is uneven, and the plates are mostly chipped, which is easy to hurt your hands. And it was very cold, there was no air conditioning, so friends who plan to go there in winter must wear down jackets when eating breakfast. After breakfast, I returned to the room and started to hear the sound of electric drills and hammers. I coordinated with the hotel again, but it was still not resolved. Their process is that the customer service gives feedback to the manager, the manager gives feedback to the construction unit, the construction unit gives feedback to the contractor, the contractor finds the workers again, and the workers still insist on drilling. I had no choice but to complain to Ctrip and change the room. Here are some suggestions.
1. The hotel facilities are good, and the environment is like a new start-up
2. The service needs a lot of room for improvement. We checked in at 10 o'clock on Friday night, and there are still many vacant rooms and rooms in areas outside the construction. Can we give priority allocation or upgrade directly? Improve the experience to a higher level.
3. The breakfast is great. Can the infrastructure be improved? Have you ever seen a broken plate in a star-level hotel?
4. Can the efficiency be improved in solving customer complaints? A total of 10 calls took 2 hours to solve the problem. Can it be solved in 1 call and 2 minutes?
5. The hot and cold water signs in the rooms that have been switched are also reversed. Similar details can be checked regularly in each room.
